<div>&lt;div id=&quot;eaembedcodecontentcustom&quot;&gt;&lt;link rel=&quot;stylesheet&quot; type=&quot;text/css&quot; href=&quot;/resource/INFAKBResource/css/bootstrap-ea.css&quot; onload=&quot;fnDoKBCssRefresh(this);&quot;/&gt;&lt;style type=&quot;text/css&quot;&gt;.expert-question{color:#0069aa}.collapsing {-webkit-transition: none;transition: none;}&lt;/style&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;container&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;masthead&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;row&quot; style=&quot;padding:10px 20px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;pull-left&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;pull-right&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;bac1da00-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse in&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Upgrade Planner for MDM MDE v10.1&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span&gt;Informatica  Upgrade Planner has been designed and created by the Informatica Global Customer  Support team to provide an insight into the Informatica product upgrades. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;&lt;span&gt;This interactive self-service guide will provide you the information  required to upgrade to Master Data Management (MDM) Multidomain Edition (MDE) v10.1. In this guide, you will learn  about the new features, architectural changes and steps to upgrade. Additionally, it  includes different types of upgrade and best practices to follow during the upgrade cycle.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Upgrade process consists of the following phases:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Perform the pre-upgrade tasks&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade Hub store&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade Hub Server&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade Process server&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Perform the post-upgrade tasks&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Upgrade steps may involve additional steps based on the version you are upgrading from. To start with the upgrade, let us understand your existing implementation.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Note: It is always recommended to run the upgrade on a small copy of production data in the development environment before you upgrade the production.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Please select your existing MDM version...&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#bac423f0-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#bac1da00-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backbac423f0-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4').attr('href', '#bac1da00-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#bac1da00-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backbacc8860-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4').attr('href', '#bac1da00-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;9.6.x&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#7b1cc770-9e64-11e5-9198-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#bac1da00-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back7b1cc770-9e64-11e5-9198-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#bac1da00-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;10.0&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;bb0a7bc1-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;After You Upgrade&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;The following are the list of tasks to be performed after the upgrade:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Restart the MDM Hub environment involving database, application server.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Migrate Databases to IBM DB2 with Oracle-compatibility Disabled - Please refer to&amp;nbsp;&lt;a title=&quot;971Upgradeguide&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Upgrade guide&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for detailed steps&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update the references to Deprecated features.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Regenerate the match tokens.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Validate the upgraded metadata:   </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Validate metadata&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Resolve metadata validation messages&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run the readiness report&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Implement the updated user exit methods.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade SiperianClient library classes for the EJB protocol.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update Server properties related to Entity view and Data view&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS (if applicable):   </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Adding users to Application server for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS URNs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrading MDM workflows for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure MDM Identity service&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update Task configuration for BE based AVOS adapter&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update AVOS .BPEL files in case of custom workflows&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Sanity tests on:&amp;nbsp;   </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;IDD applications&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hub console and batch jobs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Custom code&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;IDD - AVOS integration&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Important Note&lt;/strong&gt;: Informatica recommends that you migrate to the ActiveVOS workflow adapter based on business entities. Informatica will continue to support the Siperian workflow adapter, but it will become obsolete and Informatica will drop support in a future release.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Process Server Installation&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Process server installation involves the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Process server      application deployment&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Integrating      external cleanse engines&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Post      installation tasks such as:   </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Incase of       cluster, deploy the process server application on each node&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure       process server for multi-threading&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure       Cleanse and Match operations&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure the       external cleanse engine&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Refer the&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;installation guide&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for detailed steps on each of the activity.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Does your implementation involve any external cleanse engine?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Remote Upgrade - New Installation&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Remote upgrade is a brand new installation on new machine with all the supported PAM components.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If the machine or box is for Hub Store, then a supported OS, database version are to be installed on this machine.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If the machine or box is a Hub Server or Process Server, then a supported OS and version, application server version are to be installed on this machine.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Once the machine is ready with all the PAM compliant components, MDM installation/upgrade involves the following components in the mentioned order:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hub Store&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hub Server&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Process Server&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Shall we proceed with the Hub Store installation?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Hub Server Upgrade&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Pre-requisites&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hub Store upgrade has to be completed.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Incase of AVOS installation, ensure that AVOS schema is created as part of Hub Store installation.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Download the installers for Informatica Platform and AVOS. Refer to &lt;a href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/community/informatica-network/product-availability-matrices&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;PAM&lt;/a&gt; for the supported versions.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Incase of Platform installation, configure the platform properties file. Refer the &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Installation guide&lt;/a&gt; or download the sample properties file mentioned in the following KB article:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/14/306931.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: What are the two files required to install Informatica Platform during MDM 10.0 installation? (KB 306931)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Shall we proceed with the Hub Server upgrade?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Hub Store Upgrade&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Hub Store upgrade involves the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Master Database Upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;One or more Operational Reference Store (ORS) upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Refer to Upgrade guide for the detailed steps on upgrading Hub Store. You can download the upgrade guide from&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;a title=&quot;Informatica Network&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Informatica Network&lt;/a&gt;. Before you upgrade the Hub store, ensure that database version and OS are v10.1 &lt;a href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/community/informatica-network/product-availability-matrices&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;PAM&lt;/a&gt; compliant.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;MDM v10.1 has a tighter integration with Informatica BPM engine (ActiveVOS). To install AVOS server, you need to create AVOS schema which is a pre-requisite for AVOS installation. Refer the &quot;Create an Informatica AVOS Schema&quot; section in the Installation guide for the steps involved in creating AVOS schema.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;After successfully completing your Hub Store upgrade, lets move on to Hub Server installation.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Shall we proceed to the Hub Server upgrade?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Process server application deployment.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Integrating and/or upgrading external cleanse engines.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Post upgrade tasks such as:  </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Incase of cluster, deploy the process server application on each node&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure process server for multi-threading&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure Cleanse and Match operations&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure the external cleanse engine&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Refer the&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;installation guide&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for detailed steps on each of the activity.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Does your implementation involve any external cleanse engine?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; With this integration, data is moved to Staging tables in one step rather than moving to ETL and then pushing to Staging table.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;If you want to install Platform as part of the Hub Server installation, perform the following steps:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Download the Informatica Platform installers and provide the installer location.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Provide the sample properties file as Platform installation will be a silent installation as part of Hub Server. &lt;br /&gt;Refer the following KB article for the list of files required for Platform installation:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/14/306931.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: What are the two files required to install Informatica Platform during MDM 10.0 installation? (KB 306931)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Refer the following KB article for troubleshooting any platform installation failures:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/14/306941.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: How to troubleshoot Silent installation of Informatica Platform when installed through MDM 10.0 installers? (KB 306941)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Refer the following KB article to check the platform installation status:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/14/306938.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: How to confirm if Informatica Platform has been installed successfully when installed through MDM 10.0 install? (KB 306938)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Refer the&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;installation guide&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for more information on the installation steps.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;No&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;if you do not want to install Informatica Platform as part of Hub Server.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Shall we move on to Hub Server post installation tasks?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;After You Upgrade&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;The following are the list of tasks to be performed after the upgrade:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Restart the MDM Hub environment involving database, application server.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Migrate Databases to IBM DB2 with Oracle-compatibility Disabled - Refer to&amp;nbsp;&lt;a title=&quot;971Upgradeguide&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Upgrade guide&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for detailed steps&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update the references to Deprecated features.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Regenerate the match tokens.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Validate the upgraded metadata:   </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Validate metadata&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Resolve metadata validation messages&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run the readiness report&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Implement the updated user exit methods.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade SiperianClient library classes for the EJB protocol.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update Server properties related to Entity view and Data view&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS (if applicable):   </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Adding users to Application server for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS URNs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrading MDM workflows for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure MDM Identity service&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update Task configuration for BE based AVOS adapter&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update AVOS .BPEL files in case of custom workflows&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Sanity tests on:&amp;nbsp;   </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;IDD applications&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hub console and batch jobs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Custom code&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;IDD - AVOS integration&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Important Note&lt;/strong&gt;: Informatica recommends that you migrate to the ActiveVOS workflow adapter based on business entities. Informatica will continue to support the Siperian workflow adapter, but it will become obsolete and Informatica will drop support in a future release.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Hub Server Upgrade - Platform Installation&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;MDM v10.1 has a tight integration with Informatica Platform, which will allow you to combine the ETL process and MDM Stage process into one transformation. With this integration, data is moved to Staging tables in one step rather than moving to ETL and then pushing to Staging table.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;If you want to install Platform as part of the Hub Server installation, perform the following steps:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Download the Informatica Platform installers and provide the installer location.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Provide the sample properties file as Platform installation will be a silent installation as part of Hub Server. &lt;br /&gt; Refer the following KB article for the list of files required for Platform installation:&lt;br /&gt; &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/14/306931.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: What are the two files required to install Informatica Platform during MDM 10.0 installation? (KB 306931)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt; &lt;br /&gt; Refer the following KB article for troubleshooting any platform installation failures:&lt;br /&gt; &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/14/306941.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: How to troubleshoot Silent installation of Informatica Platform when installed through MDM 10.0 installers? (KB 306941)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt; &lt;br /&gt; Refer the following KB article to check the platform installation status:&lt;br /&gt; &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/14/306938.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: How to confirm if Informatica Platform has been installed successfully when installed through MDM 10.0 install? (KB 306938)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Refer the&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;installation guide&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for more information on the installation steps.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;No&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;if you do not want to install Informatica Platform as part of Hub Server.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to proceed with the Hub Server upgrade?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Hub Store Upgrade (Installation)&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Hub Store upgrade involves the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Master Database Upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;One or more Operational Reference Store (ORS) upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Refer to Upgrade guide for the detailed steps on upgrading Hub Store. You can download the upgrade guide from&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;a title=&quot;Informatica Network&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Informatica Network&lt;/a&gt;. Before you upgrade the Hub store, ensure that database version and OS are v10.1 &lt;a href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/community/informatica-network/product-availability-matrices&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;PAM&lt;/a&gt; compliant.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;MDM v10.1 has a tighter integration with Informatica BPM engine (ActiveVOS). To install AVOS server, you need to create AVOS schema which is a pre-requisite for AVOS installation. Refer the &quot;Create an Informatica AVOS Schema&quot; section in the Installation guide for the steps involved in creating AVOS schema.&lt;/p&gt;</div>

class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;After You Upgrade&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;The following are the list of tasks to be performed after the upgrade:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Restart the MDM Hub environment involving database, application server.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Migrate Databases to IBM DB2 with Oracle-compatibility Disabled - Please refer to&amp;nbsp;&lt;a title=&quot;971Upgradeguide&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Upgrade guide&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for detailed steps&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update the references to Deprecated features.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Regenerate the match tokens.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Validate the upgraded metadata:   </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Validate metadata&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Resolve metadata validation messages&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run the readiness report&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Implement the updated user exit methods.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade SiperianClient library classes for the EJB protocol.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update Server properties related to Entity view and Data view&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS (if applicable):   </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Adding users to Application server for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS URNs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrading MDM workflows for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure MDM Identity service&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update Task configuration for BE based AVOS adapter&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update AVOS .BPEL files in case of custom workflows&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Sanity tests on:&amp;nbsp;   </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;IDD applications&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hub console and batch jobs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Custom code&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;IDD - AVOS integration&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Important Note&lt;/strong&gt;: Informatica recommends that you migrate to the ActiveVOS workflow adapter based on business entities. Informatica will continue to support the Siperian workflow adapter, but it will become obsolete and Informatica will drop support in a future release.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; <div>&lt;li&gt;Get the MDM      license if your implementation involves additional components such as      Platform integration, Informatica BPM (ActiveVOS) etc.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Get the      installers from Informatica support by raising a shipping request asking      for:&amp;nbsp;   </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;ActiveVOS       installers - 9.2.4.1&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Platform       installers - 9.6.1 HF3&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;(Request shipping team explicitly to       provide MDM-specific Vibe installers)&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade the      Operating System (OS), application server and database server versions as      per v10.1 &lt;a href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/community/informatica-network/product-availability-matrices&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;PAM&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Shall we move on to the upgrade process?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Process server application deployment&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Integrating external cleanse engines&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Post installation tasks such as:   </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Incase of cluster, deploy the process server application on each node&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure process server for multi-threading&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure Cleanse and Match operations&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure the external cleanse engine&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Refer the &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;installation guide&lt;/a&gt; for detailed steps on each of the activity.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Does your implementation involve any external cleanse engine?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Master Database      Upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;One or more      Operational Reference Store (ORS) upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Refer to Upgrade guide for the detailed steps on upgrading Hub Store. You can download the upgrade guide from&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;a title=&quot;Informatica Network&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Informatica Network&lt;/a&gt;. Before you upgrade the Hub store, ensure that database version and OS are v10.1 &lt;a href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/community/informatica-network/product-availability-matrices&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;PAM&lt;/a&gt; compliant.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;MDM v10.1 has a tighter integration with Informatica BPM engine (ActiveVOS). To install AVOS server, you need to create AVOS schema which is a pre-requisite for AVOS installation. Refer the &quot;Create an Informatica AVOS Schema&quot; section in the Installation guide for the steps involved in creating AVOS schema.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;If you want to install ActiveVOS as part of the Hub Server installation, perform the following steps:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Download the AVOS installers and provide the installers location.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Provide the details of AVOS schema as part of Hub Store creation.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Provide the URL to access AVOS web services.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Refer the&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;installation guide&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for more information on the installation steps.&lt;/p&gt;</div>

class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;7b1cc770-9e64-11e5-9198-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Overview on Upgrade - v10.0 to v10.1&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;From MDM v10.0 to v10.1, there are no major architectural changes. Provisioning tool is introduced to help configuring Business entity, BES, Start page etc., and Informatica BPM integration with MDM through Identity service supporting BE workflows and Subject area workflows are the key highlights. Following are the new additions.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;New features from v10.0 to v10.1:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Provisioning      tool&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Tighter      integration with Informatica BPM (formerly called as ActiveVOS)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Business Entity      views &amp;amp; Transformations&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;REST API      Business Entity Service calls&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;IDD improvements      - Wildcard search, Search string suggestions &amp;amp; Jaspsersoft reports in      Start page&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade with      Zero Downtime (ZDT) - supported for Oracle &amp;amp; IBM DB2 databases&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Task Manager in      IDD&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Batch jobs on child base objects can run in parallel&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Loading multiple versions of records in a batch job&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Behavioral changes from v10.0 to v10.1:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Tokenization      process&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica BPM      integration (now, through Identity service)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Deprecated Features:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;EJB2 Protocol&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;IBM ILOG Charts in IDD&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hub store installation in Oracle 12c environment with Multi-tenant Oracle containers&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to move on to the pre-requisites?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <div>&lt;li&gt;Hub Store upgrade has to be completed.&lt;/li&gt;</div>

(KB 306931)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>

class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Overview on Upgrade - 9.5.x to v10.1&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;From MDM 9.5.x to v10.1, there are major architectural changes. One of the intermediate version had moved the consolidation logic from database tier to application server tier for better performance and supportability of new database (here, SQLServer). Following are the new additions:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;New features from 9.5.x to v10.1:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Provisioning      tool&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Tighter      integration with Informatica BPM (formerly called as ActiveVOS)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Business Entity      views &amp;amp; Transformations&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;REST API      Business Entity Service calls&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;IDD improvements      - Wildcard search, Search string suggestions &amp;amp; Jaspsersoft reports in      Start page&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade with      Zero Downtime (ZDT) - supported for Oracle &amp;amp; IBM DB2 databases&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Task Manager in      IDD&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Language      selection in Hub console&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Capability to      have multiple MDM Hub Master databases&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica      Platform staging&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Business Entity      &amp;amp; Business Entity Services&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Business Entity      view&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Smart Search&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Proximity search&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Data encryption&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Database      agnostic release&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Timeline      granularity&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Change in      Tokenization logic&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Support for Jasper      Reports in IDD&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Behavioral changes from 9.5.x to v10.1:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Tokenization process&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica BPM integration (now, through Identity service)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hard Delete      Detection - now to be enabled in Java user exits&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Changes in post      merge, pre and post unmerge user exits&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;User exit SIF      Framework&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;IBM DB2 setup -      disable Oracle-compatibility mode&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Batch unmerge -      moved to Java&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Deprecated Features:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Database user      exits&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;EJB2 for SIF Framework&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Link style Base Object&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;IBM ILOG Charts in IDD&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hub store installation in Oracle 12c environment with Multitenant Oracle containers&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Proxy role&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to move on to the pre-requisites?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#bae0d3b0-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#bac33990-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backbae0d3b0-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4').attr('href', '#bac33990-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Overview on Upgrade - From 9.6.x to v10.1&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;From MDM 9.6.x to v10.1, there are no major architectural changes. Version 9.6 being a database agnostic release, it only supports SQLServer database. Later release such as 9.6.1 and 9.6.1 HotFix 1, supports other databases also (Oracle and DB2). Following are the new additions.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;New features from 9.6.x to v10.1:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Provisioning      tool&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Tighter      integration with Informatica BPM (formerly called as ActiveVOS)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Business Entity      views &amp;amp; Transformations&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;REST API      Business Entity Service calls&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;IDD improvements      - Wildcard search, Search string suggestions &amp;amp; Jaspsersoft reports in      Start page&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade with      Zero Downtime (ZDT) - supported for Oracle &amp;amp; IBM DB2 databases&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Task Manager in IDD&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Batch jobs on child base objects can run in parallel&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Loading multiple versions of records in a batch job&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Language      selection in Hub console&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Capability to      have multiple MDM Hub Master databases&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica      Platform staging&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Business Entity      &amp;amp; Business Entity Services&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Business Entity view&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Smart Search&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Proximity search&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Data encryption&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Behavioral changes from 9.6.x to v10.1:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;SIF - EJB2      Protocols&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Tokenization      process&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica BPM      integration (now, through Identity service)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Deprecated Features:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;EJB2 for SIF Framework&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Link style Base Object&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;IBM ILOG Charts in IDD&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hub store installation in Oracle 12c environment with Multitenant Oracle containers&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Proxy role&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to move on to the pre-requisites?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica Data Quality - 9.0.x, 9.1 HotFix 3, 9.5, 9.5.1, 9.6 and 9.6.1&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica Name3 - 9.5.3 HotFix 1&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica AddressDoctor - 5.8&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Trillium - 14 and 15&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To upgrade AddressDoctor from earlier versions to 5.4.1, refer the following KB article (steps remains the same even though MDM version pointing in the KB is older):&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/3/Pages/141285.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;HOW TO: Upgrade the version of AddressDoctor from 5.2.5.624 to 5.2.7.785 in MDM 9.1.0 (KB 141285)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Shall we move on to post upgrade/install steps?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;After You Upgrade&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;The following are the list of tasks to be performed after the upgrade:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Restart the MDM Hub environment involving database, application server.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Migrate Databases to IBM DB2 with Oracle-compatibility Disabled - Refer to&amp;nbsp;&lt;a title=&quot;971Upgradeguide&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Upgrade guide&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for detailed steps&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update the references to Deprecated features.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Regenerate the match tokens.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Validate the upgraded metadata:     </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Validate metadata&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Resolve metadata validation messages&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run the readiness report&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Implement the updated user exit methods.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade SiperianClient library classes for the EJB protocol.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update Server properties related to Entity view and Data view&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS (if applicable):     </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Adding users to Application server for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS URNs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrading MDM workflows for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure MDM Identity service&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update Task configuration for BE based AVOS adapter&lt;span&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update AVOS .BPEL files in case of custom workflows&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Sanity tests on:&amp;nbsp;     </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;IDD applications&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hub console and batch jobs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Custom code&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;IDD - AVOS integration&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;Also, MDM v10.1 has a tight integration with ActiveVOS BPM engine. IDD native workflow is replaced by the ActiveVOS BPM capabilities.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;If you want to install ActiveVOS as part of the Hub Server installation, perform the following steps:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;Provide the details of AVOS schema as part of Hub Store creation.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Provide the URL to access AVOS web services.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>

With this integration, data is moved to Staging tables in one step rather than moving to ETL and then pushing to Staging table.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;If you want to install Platform as part of the Hub Server installation, perform the following steps:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Download the Informatica Platform installers and provide the installer location.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Provide the sample properties file as Platform installation will be a silent installation as part of Hub Server. &lt;br /&gt;Refer the following KB article for the list of files required for Platform installation:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/14/306931.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: What are the two files required to install Informatica Platform during MDM 10.0 installation? (KB 306931)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Refer the following KB article for troubleshooting any platform installation failures:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/14/306941.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: How to troubleshoot Silent installation of Informatica Platform when installed through MDM 10.0 installers? (KB 306941)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Refer the following KB article to check the platform installation status:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/14/306938.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: How to confirm if Informatica Platform has been installed successfully when installed through MDM 10.0 install? (KB 306938)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Refer the&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;installation guide&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for more information on the installation steps.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;No&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;if you do not want to install Informatica Platform as part of Hub Server.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Shall we move on to Hub Server post installation tasks?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Master Database Upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;One or more Operational Reference Store (ORS) upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Refer to Upgrade guide for the detailed steps on upgrading Hub Store. You can download the upgrade guide from&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;a title=&quot;Informatica Network&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Informatica Network&lt;/a&gt;. Before you upgrade the Hub store, ensure that database version and OS are v10.1 &lt;a href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/community/informatica-network/product-availability-matrices&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;PAM&lt;/a&gt; compliant.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;MDM v10.1 has a tighter integration with Informatica BPM engine (ActiveVOS). To install AVOS server, you need to create AVOS schema which is a pre-requisite for AVOS installation. Refer the &quot;Create an Informatica AVOS Schema&quot; section in the Installation guide for the steps involved in creating AVOS schema.&lt;/p&gt;</div>

class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Hub Server Installation - Platform Installation&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;MDM v10.1 has a tight integration with Informatica Platform, which will allow you to combine the ETL process and MDM Stage process into one transformation. With this integration, data is moved to Staging tables in one step rather than moving to ETL and then pushing to Staging table.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;If you want to install Platform as part of the Hub Server installation, perform the following steps:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Download the Informatica Platform installers and provide the installer location.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Provide the sample properties file as Platform installation will be a silent installation as part of Hub Server.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt; &lt;br /&gt; Refer the following KB article for the list of files required for Platform installation:&lt;br /&gt; &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/14/306931.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: What are the two files required to install Informatica Platform during MDM 10.0 installation? (KB 306941)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt; &lt;br /&gt; Refer the following KB article to check the platform installation status:&lt;br /&gt; &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/14/306938.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: How to confirm if Informatica Platform has been installed successfully when installed through MDM 10.0 install? (KB 306938)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>

If the box is a Hub server or Process server, then we need to upgrade to a supported Operating System and version, Application server version.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Once the box is ready with all the PAM compliant components, MDM upgrade involves the following components in the mentioned order:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hub Store&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hub Server&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Process Server&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>

Before you upgrade the Hub store, ensure that database version and OS are v10.1 &lt;a href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/community/informatica-network/product-availability-matrices&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;PAM&lt;/a&gt; compliant.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;MDM v10.1 has a tighter integration with Informatica BPM engine (ActiveVOS). To install AVOS server, you need to create AVOS schema, which is a pre-requisite for AVOS installation. Refer the &quot;Create an Informatica AVOS Schema&quot; section in the Installation guide for the steps involved in creating AVOS schema.&lt;/p&gt;</div>

IDD native workflow is replaced by the ActiveVOS BPM capabilities.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;If you want to install ActiveVOS as part of the Hub Server installation, perform the following steps:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Download the AVOS installers and provide the installers location.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Provide the details of AVOS schema as part of Hub Store creation.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Provide the URL to access AVOS web services.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Refer the &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;installation guide&lt;/a&gt; for more information on the installation steps.&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Master Database Upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;One or more Operational Reference Store (ORS) upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Refer to Upgrade guide for the detailed steps on upgrading Hub Store. You can download the upgrade guide from&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;a title=&quot;Informatica Network&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Informatica Network&lt;/a&gt;. Before you upgrade the Hub store, ensure that database version and OS are v10.1 &lt;a href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/community/informatica-network/product-availability-matrices&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;PAM&lt;/a&gt; compliant.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;MDM v10.1 has a tighter integration with Informatica BPM engine (ActiveVOS). To install AVOS server, you need to create AVOS schema which is a pre-requisite for AVOS installation. Refer the &quot;Create an Informatica AVOS Schema&quot; section in the Installation guide for the steps involved in creating AVOS schema.&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Restart the MDM      Hub environment involving database, application server.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Migrate      Databases to IBM DB2 with Oracle-compatibility Disabled - Refer      the &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Upgrade      guide&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for detailed steps&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update the      references to Deprecated features.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Regenerate the      match tokens.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Validate the      upgraded metadata:   </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Validate       metadata&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Resolve       metadata validation messages&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run the       readiness report&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Implement the      updated user exit methods.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade      SiperianClient library classes for the EJB protocol.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update Server      properties related to Entity view and Data view&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS      (if applicable):   </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Adding users to       Application server for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS       URNs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrading MDM       workflows for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure MDM       Identity service&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update Task       configuration for BE based AVOS adapter&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update AVOS       .BPEL files in case of custom workflows&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Sanity tests      on:&amp;nbsp;   </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;IDD       applications&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hub console and       batch jobs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Custom code&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;IDD - AVOS       integration&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica Data Quality - 9.0.x, 9.1 HotFix 3, 9.5, 9.5.1, 9.6 and 9.6.1&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica Name3 - 9.5.3 HotFix 1&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica AddressDoctor - 5.8&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Trillium - 14 and 15&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Process server application deployment.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Integrating and/or upgrading external cleanse engines.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Post upgrade tasks such as:   </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Incase of cluster, deploy the process server application on each node&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure process server for multi-threading&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure Cleanse and Match operations&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure the external cleanse engine&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Refer the &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;installation guide&lt;/a&gt; for detailed steps on each of the activity.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Does your implementation involve any external cleanse engine?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backbaef0480-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#baef0480-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; href=&quot;#bac1da00-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#baef0480-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;bac423f0-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Overview on Upgrade - 9.0.1/9.1 to v10.1&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;From MDM 9.0.1/9.1 to v10.1, there are major architectural changes. One of the intermediate version has moved the consolidation logic from database tier to application server tier for better performance and supportability of new database (here, SQLServer). Following are the new additions:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;New features from 9.0.1/9.1 to v10.1:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Provisioning      tool&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Tighter      integration with Informatica BPM (formerly called as ActiveVOS)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Business Entity      views &amp;amp; Transformations&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;REST API      Business Entity Service calls&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;IDD improvements      - Wildcard search, Search string suggestions &amp;amp; Jaspsersoft reports in      Start page&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade with      Zero Downtime (ZDT) - supported for Oracle &amp;amp; IBM DB2 databases&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Task Manager in      IDD&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Language      selection in Hub console&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Capability to      have multiple MDM Hub Master databases&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica      Platform staging&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Business Entity      &amp;amp; Business Entity Services&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Business Entity      view&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Smart Search&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Proximity search&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Data encryption&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Database      agnostic release&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Timeline      granularity&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Change in      Tokenization logic&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Support for      Jasper Reports in IDD&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Timeline&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Behavioral changes from 9.0.1/9.1 to v10.1:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Tokenization process&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica BPM integration (now, through Identity service)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Foreign Key      merge lineage is maintained in XREF table&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Merge lineage is      maintained in XREF table&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;HM Relationship      effective dates are replaced by Period_Start_Date and Period_End_Date&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hard Delete      Detection - now to be enabled in Java user exits&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Changes in post      merge, pre and post unmerge user exits&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;User exit SIF      Framework&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;IBM DB2 setup -      disable Oracle-compatibility mode&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Batch unmerge -      moved to Java&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Deprecated Features:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Database user exits&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;EJB2 for SIF Framework&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Link style Base Object&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;IBM ILOG Charts in IDD&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hub store installation in Oracle 12c environment with Multitenant Oracle containers&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Proxy role&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to move on to the pre-requisites?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Hub Server Upgrade - AVOS Installation&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;To start with the Hub Server upgrade, run the Hub Server installer and point to the upgraded application server and upgraded Hub Store. Point to the existing MDM installation folder while running the installer to upgrade Hub Server on to v10.1.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Also, MDM v10.1 has a tight integration with ActiveVOS BPM engine. IDD native workflow is replaced by the ActiveVOS BPM capabilities.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;If you want to install ActiveVOS as part of the Hub Server installation, perform the following steps:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Download the AVOS installers and provide the installers location.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Provide the details of AVOS schema as part of Hub Store creation.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Provide the URL to access AVOS web services.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Refer the&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;installation guide&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for more information on the installation steps.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;No&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;if you do not want to install ActiveVOS as part of Hub server.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to proceed with the Hub Server upgrade?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Hub Server Installation&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Pre-requisites&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hub Store installation has to be completed.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Incase of AVOS installation, ensure that AVOS schema is created as part of Hub Store installation.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Create AVOS Administrative User &amp;amp; Admin User in Application server. Refer Application server specific Installation guide available at &lt;a title=&quot;Informatica Network&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Informatica Network.&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Download the installers for Informatica Platform and AVOS. Refer &lt;a href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/community/informatica-network/product-availability-matrices&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;PAM&lt;/a&gt; for the supported versions.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Incase of Platform installation, configure the platform properties file. Refer the &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Installation guide&lt;/a&gt; or download the sample properties file mentioned in the following KB article:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/14/306931.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: What are the two files required to install Informatica Platform during MDM 10.0 installation? (KB 306931)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Shall we proceed with the Hub Server installation?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica Data Quality - 9.0.x, 9.1 HotFix 3, 9.5, 9.5.1, 9.6 and 9.6.1&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica Name3 - 9.5.3 HotFix 1&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica AddressDoctor - 5.8&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Trillium - 14 and 15&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If the machine      or box is for Hub Store, then a supported OS, database version are to be      installed on this machine.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If the machine      or box is a Hub Server or Process Server, then a supported OS and version,      application server version are to be installed on this machine.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Once the machine is ready with all the PAM compliant components, MDM installation/upgrade involves the following components in the mentioned order:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hub Store&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hub Server&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Process Server&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Shall we proceed with the Hub Store installation?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <div>&lt;p&gt;If you want to install ActiveVOS as part of the Hub Server installation, perform the following steps:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;Provide the URL to access AVOS web services.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>

class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Before You Upgrade&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Before upgrading to v10.1, follow these best practices for a smoother upgrade:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Memory Settings &lt;em&gt;(JVM memory configuration has to be increased to accommodate multiple integrations with MDM)&lt;/em&gt; - Refer to Installation guide&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Backup the implementation.         </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Backup the schema - Database backup&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Backup IDD application(s)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Backup customizations such as user exit code&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Backup external cleanse engine customizations&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Backup custom objects such as custom stored procedures, custom indexes etc.,&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Validate the metadata.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Resolve data issues that affect the upgrade.         </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Generate the readiness report&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Fix the data issues by running a script&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Resolve manual mandatory data issues&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;After following the best practices, proceed with the upgrade type that is applicable for your MDM implementation.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Want to know more about the upgrade types?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <div>&lt;li&gt;Master Database Upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;One or more Operational Reference Store (ORS) upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;a title=&quot;Informatica Network&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Informatica Network&lt;/a&gt;. Refer the &quot;Create an Informatica AVOS Schema&quot; section in the Installation guide for the steps involved in creating AVOS schema.&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;MDM v10.1 has a tighter integration with Informatica BPM engine (ActiveVOS). To install AVOS server, you need to create AVOS schema which is a pre-requisite for AVOS installation. Refer the &quot;Create an Informatica AVOS Schema&quot; section in the Installation guide for the steps involved in creating AVOS schema.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;After successfully completing your Hub Store upgrade, lets move on to Hub Server installation.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Shall we proceed to the Hub Server installation?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backbac73130-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#bac73130-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;After You Upgrade&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;The following are the list of tasks to be performed after the upgrade:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Restart the MDM Hub environment involving database, application server.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Migrate Databases to IBM DB2 with Oracle-compatibility Disabled - Refer to&amp;nbsp;&lt;a title=&quot;971Upgradeguide&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Upgrade guide&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for detailed steps&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update the references to Deprecated features.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Regenerate the match tokens.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Validate the upgraded metadata:   </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Validate metadata&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Resolve metadata validation messages&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run the readiness report&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Implement the updated user exit methods.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade SiperianClient library classes for the EJB protocol.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update Server properties related to Entity view and Data view&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS (if applicable):   </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Adding users to Application server for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS URNs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrading MDM workflows for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure MDM Identity service&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update Task configuration for BE based AVOS adapter&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update AVOS .BPEL files in case of custom workflows&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Sanity tests on:&amp;nbsp;   </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;IDD applications&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hub console and batch jobs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Custom code&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;IDD - AVOS integration&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Important Note&lt;/strong&gt;: Informatica recommends that you migrate to the ActiveVOS workflow adapter based on business entities. Informatica will continue to support the Siperian workflow adapter, but it will become obsolete and Informatica will drop support in a future release.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hub Store installation has to be completed.&lt;/li&gt;</div>

class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Types of Upgrade&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Upgrade steps differ based on the type of upgrade involved.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The following are the two types of upgrade:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;On-Premise&lt;/strong&gt;: This type of upgrade uses the same machine or box by upgrading the OS, application server version or database server version etc., to be compliant with v10.1 PAM.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Remote&lt;/strong&gt;:&amp;nbsp;This type of upgrade involves a new machine or box with all the PAM compliant OS, application server or database server etc.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt; &lt;ol&gt; &lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Select the type of upgrade...&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade the Operating System (OS), application server and database server versions as per v10.1 &lt;a href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/community/informatica-network/product-availability-matrices&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;PAM&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Shall we move on to the upgrade process?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica Data Quality - 9.0.x, 9.1 HotFix 3, 9.5, 9.5.1, 9.6 and 9.6.1&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica Name3 - 9.5.3 HotFix 1&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica AddressDoctor - 5.8&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Trillium - 14 and 15&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>

class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Before You Upgrade&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Before upgrading to v10.1, follow these best practices for a smoother upgrade:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Memory Settings&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;(JVM memory configuration has to be increased to accommodate multiple integrations with MDM)&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;- Refer to Installation guide&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Backup the implementation.  </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Backup the schema - Database backup&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Backup IDD application(s)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Backup customizations such as user exit code&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Backup external cleanse engine customizations&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Backup custom objects such as custom stored procedures, custom indexes etc.,&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Validate the metadata.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Resolve data issues that affect the upgrade.  </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Generate the readiness report&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Fix the data issues by running a script&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Resolve manual mandatory data issues&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;After following the best practices, proceed with the upgrade type that is applicable for your MDM implementation.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Want to know more about the Upgrade types?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot;
