class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Types of Upgrade&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Upgrade steps differ based on the type of upgrade involved.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The following are the two types of upgrade:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;On-Premise&lt;/strong&gt;: This type of upgrade uses the same machine or box by upgrading the OS, application server version or database server version etc., to be compliant with v10.1 PAM.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Remote&lt;/strong&gt;:&amp;nbsp;This type of upgrade involves a new machine or box with all the PAM compliant OS, application server or database server etc.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt; &lt;ol&gt; &lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Select the type of upgrade...&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <div>&lt;li&gt;Provide the details of AVOS schema as part of Hub Store creation.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Provide the URL to access AVOS web services.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;Hub Server&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Master Database Upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;One or more Operational Reference Store (ORS) upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Refer to Upgrade guide for the detailed steps on upgrading Hub Store. You can download the upgrade guide from&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;a title=&quot;Informatica Network&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Informatica Network&lt;/a&gt;. Before you upgrade the Hub store, ensure that database version and OS are v10.1 &lt;a href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/community/informatica-network/product-availability-matrices&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;PAM&lt;/a&gt; compliant.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;MDM v10.1 has a tighter integration with Informatica BPM engine (ActiveVOS). To install AVOS server, you need to create AVOS schema which is a pre-requisite for AVOS installation. Refer the &quot;Create an Informatica AVOS Schema&quot; section in the Installation guide for the steps involved in creating AVOS schema.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;After successfully completing your Hub Store upgrade, lets move on to Hub Server installation.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Shall we proceed to the Hub Server upgrade?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <div>&lt;p&gt;The following are the two types of upgrade:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;On-Premise&lt;/strong&gt;: This type of upgrade uses the same machine or box by upgrading the OS, application server version or database server version etc., to be compliant with v10.1 PAM.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Remote&lt;/strong&gt;:&amp;nbsp;This type of upgrade involves a new machine or box with all the PAM compliant OS, application server or database server etc.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt; &lt;ol&gt; &lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Select the type of upgrade...&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Before You Upgrade&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Before upgrading to v10.1, follow these best practices for a smoother upgrade:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Memory Settings&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;(JVM memory configuration has to be increased to accommodate multiple integrations with MDM)&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;- Refer to Installation guide.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Backup the implementation.</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Backup the schema - Database backup&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Backup IDD application(s)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Backup customizations such as user exit code&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Backup external cleanse engine customizations&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Backup custom objects such as custom stored procedures, custom indexes etc.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Validate the metadata.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Resolve data issues that affect the upgrade.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Generate the readiness report.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Fix the data issues by running a script.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Resolve manual mandatory data issues.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;After following the best practices, proceed with the upgrade type that is applicable for your MDM implementation.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Want to know more about the upgrade types?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If the machine or box is for Hub Store, then a supported OS, database version are to be installed on this machine.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If the machine or box is a Hub Server or Process Server, then a supported OS and version, application server version are to be installed on this machine.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Once the machine is ready with all the PAM compliant components, MDM installation/upgrade involves the following components in the mentioned order:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hub Store&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hub Server&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Process Server&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt; &lt;ol&gt; &lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Shall we proceed with the Hub Store installation?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <div>&lt;p&gt;If you want to install ActiveVOS as part of the Hub Server installation, perform the following steps:&lt;/p&gt;</div>

With this integration, data is moved to Staging tables in one step rather than moving to ETL and then pushing to Staging table.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;If you want to install Platform as part of the Hub Server installation, perform the following steps:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Download the Informatica Platform installers and provide the installer location.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Provide the sample properties file as Platform installation will be a silent installation as part of Hub Server. &lt;br /&gt;Refer the following KB article for the list of files required for Platform installation:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/14/306931.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: What are the two files required to install Informatica Platform during MDM 10.0 installation? class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;bac27640-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Overview on Upgrade - 9.7.x to v10.1&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;From MDM 9.7.x to v10.1, there are no major architectural changes. Optional features of integrating Platform to MDM and tighter integration with Informatica BPM (formerly called as ActiveVOS) are the key highlights of this release. Following are the new additions:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;New features from 9.7.x to v10.1:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Provisioning tool&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Tighter integration with Informatica BPM (formerly called as ActiveVOS)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Business Entity views &amp;amp; Transformations&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;REST API Business Entity Service calls&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;IDD improvements - Wildcard search, Search string suggestions &amp;amp; Jaspsersoft reports in Start page&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade with Zero Downtime (ZDT) - supported for Oracle &amp;amp; IBM DB2 databases&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Task Manager in IDD&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Batch jobs on child base objects can run in parallel&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Loading multiple versions of records in a batch job&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Language selection in Hub console&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Capability to have multiple MDM Hub Master databases&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica Platform staging&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Business Entity &amp;amp; Business Entity Services&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Smart Search&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Behavioral changes from 9.7.x to v10.1:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Default Proxy role&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;SIF - EJB2 Protocols&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Tokenization process&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica BPM integration (now, through Identity service)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Deprecated Features:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;EJB2 for SIF Framework&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Link style Base Object&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;IBM ILOG Charts in IDD&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hub store installation in Oracle 12c environment with Multitenant Oracle containers&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to move on to the pre-requisites?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; With this integration, data is moved to Staging tables in one step rather than moving to ETL and then pushing to Staging table.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;If you want to install Platform as part of the Hub Server installation, perform the following steps:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Download the Informatica Platform installers and provide the installer location.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Provide the sample properties file as Platform installation will be a silent installation as part of Hub Server. &lt;br /&gt;Refer the following KB article for the list of files required for Platform installation:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/14/306931.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: What are the two files required to install Informatica Platform during MDM 10.0 installation? (KB 306931)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Refer the following KB article for troubleshooting any platform installation failures:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/14/306941.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: How to troubleshoot Silent installation of Informatica Platform when installed through MDM 10.0 installers? (KB 306941)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Refer the following KB article to check the platform installation status:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/14/306938.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: How to confirm if Informatica Platform has been installed successfully when installed through MDM 10.0 install? (KB 306938)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Download the Informatica Platform installers and provide the installer location.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Provide the sample properties file as Platform installation will be a silent installation as part of Hub Server. &lt;br /&gt;Refer the following KB article for the list of files required for Platform installation:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/14/306931.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: What are the two files required to install Informatica Platform during MDM 10.0 installation? (KB 306931)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Refer the following KB article for troubleshooting any platform installation failures:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/14/306941.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: How to troubleshoot Silent installation of Informatica Platform when installed through MDM 10.0 installers? (KB 306941)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Refer the following KB article to check the platform installation status:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/14/306938.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: How to confirm if Informatica Platform has been installed successfully when installed through MDM 10.0 install? (KB 306938)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Refer the &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;installation guide&lt;/a&gt; for more information on the installation steps.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;No&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;if you do not want to install Informatica Platform as part of Hub Server.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Shall we move on to Hub Server post installation tasks?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Before You Upgrade&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Before upgrading to v10.1, follow these best practices for a smoother upgrade:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Memory Settings&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;(JVM memory configuration has to be increased to accommodate multiple integrations with MDM)&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;- Refer to Installation guide&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Backup the implementation.  </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Backup the schema - Database backup&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Backup IDD application(s)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Backup customizations such as user exit code&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Backup external cleanse engine customizations&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Backup custom objects such as custom stored procedures, custom indexes etc.,&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Validate the metadata.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Resolve data issues that affect the upgrade.  </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Generate the readiness report&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Fix the data issues by running a script&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Resolve manual mandatory data issues&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;After following the best practices, proceed with the upgrade type that is applicable for your MDM implementation.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Want to know more about the upgrade types?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Restart the MDM Hub environment involving database, application server.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Migrate Databases to IBM DB2 with Oracle-compatibility Disabled - Please refer to&amp;nbsp;&lt;a title=&quot;971Upgradeguide&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Upgrade guide&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for detailed steps&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update the references to Deprecated features.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Regenerate the match tokens.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Validate the upgraded metadata:   </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Validate metadata&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Resolve metadata validation messages&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run the readiness report&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Implement the updated user exit methods.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade SiperianClient library classes for the EJB protocol.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update Server properties related to Entity view and Data view&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS (if applicable):   </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Adding users to Application server for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS URNs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrading MDM workflows for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure MDM Identity service&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update Task configuration for BE based AVOS adapter&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update AVOS .BPEL files in case of custom workflows&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Sanity tests on:&amp;nbsp;   </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;IDD applications&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hub console and batch jobs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Custom code&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;IDD - AVOS integration&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>

If the box is a Hub server or Process server, then we need to upgrade to a supported Operating System and version, Application server version.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Once the box is ready with all the PAM compliant components, MDM upgrade involves the following components in the mentioned order:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hub Store&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hub Server&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Process Server&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Shall we proceed with the Hub Store upgrade?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Master Database Upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;One or more Operational Reference Store (ORS) upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Refer to Upgrade guide for the detailed steps on upgrading Hub Store. You can download the upgrade guide from&lt;/p&gt;</div>

Before you upgrade the Hub store, ensure that database version and OS are v10.1 &lt;a href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/community/informatica-network/product-availability-matrices&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;PAM&lt;/a&gt; compliant.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;MDM v10.1 has a tighter integration with Informatica BPM engine (ActiveVOS). To install AVOS server, you need to create AVOS schema which is a pre-requisite for AVOS installation. Refer the &quot;Create an Informatica AVOS Schema&quot; section in the Installation guide for the steps involved in creating AVOS schema.&lt;/p&gt;</div>

With this integration, data is moved to Staging tables in one step rather than moving to ETL and then pushing to Staging table.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;If you want to install Platform as part of the Hub Server installation, perform the following steps:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Download the Informatica Platform installers and provide the installer location.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Provide the sample properties file as Platform installation will be a silent installation as part of Hub Server. &lt;br /&gt;Refer the following KB article for the list of files required for Platform installation:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/14/306931.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: What are the two files required to install Informatica Platform during MDM 10.0 installation? (KB 306941)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Refer the following KB article to check the platform installation status:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/14/306938.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;FAQ: How to confirm if Informatica Platform has been installed successfully when installed through MDM 10.0 install? <div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>

class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Types of Upgrade&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Upgrade steps differ based on the type of upgrade involved. The following are the two types of upgrade:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;On-Premise&lt;/strong&gt;: This type of upgrade uses the same machine or box by upgrading the OS, application server version or database server version etc., to be compliant with v10.1 PAM.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Remote&lt;/strong&gt;:&amp;nbsp;This type of upgrade involves a new machine or box with all the PAM compliant OS, application server or database server etc.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Select the type of upgrade...&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#bae62ae0-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#bae54080-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backbae62ae0-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4').attr('href', '#bae54080-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Remote&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#baea4990-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; <div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verifying version and build number&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;For application clusters, manually deploying Hub Server application&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Manually creating data sources&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Manually creating JMS queues&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Repackaging custom jar files&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;JBoss cache configuration&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Refer the&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;installation guide&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for clear instructions on every task mentioned above.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Shall we move on to the Process Server Installation?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Remote Upgrade - New Installation&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Remote upgrade is a brand new installation on new machine with all the supported PAM components.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If the machine or box is for Hub Store, then a supported OS, database version are to be installed on this machine.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If the machine or box is a Hub Server or Process Server, then a supported OS and version, application server version are to be installed on this machine.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Once the machine or box is ready with all the PAM compliant components, MDM installation/upgrade involves the following components in the mentioned order:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hub Store&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hub Server&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Process Server&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Shall we proceed with the Hub Store installation?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;bb06ab30-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;After You Upgrade&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;The following are the list of tasks to be performed after the upgrade:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Restart the MDM Hub environment involving database, application server.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Migrate Databases to IBM DB2 with Oracle-compatibility Disabled - Please refer to&amp;nbsp;&lt;a title=&quot;971Upgradeguide&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Upgrade guide&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for detailed steps&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update the references to Deprecated features.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Regenerate the match tokens.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Validate the upgraded metadata:   </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Validate metadata&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Resolve metadata validation messages&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run the readiness report&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Implement the updated user exit methods.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade SiperianClient library classes for the EJB protocol.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update Server properties related to Entity view and Data view&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS (if applicable):   </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Adding users to Application server for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS URNs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrading MDM workflows for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure MDM Identity service&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update Task configuration for BE based AVOS adapter&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update AVOS .BPEL files in case of custom workflows&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Sanity tests on:&amp;nbsp;   </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;IDD applications&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hub console and batch jobs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Custom code&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;IDD - AVOS integration&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Important Note&lt;/strong&gt;: Informatica recommends that you migrate to the ActiveVOS workflow adapter based on business entities. Informatica will continue to support the Siperian workflow adapter, but it will become obsolete and Informatica will drop support in a future release.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backbb06ab30-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#bb06ab30-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#bac1da00-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#bb06ab30-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;bb023e61-94eb-11e5-9ce8-bc764e11d2f4&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Before You Upgrade&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Before upgrading to v10.1, follow these best practices for a smoother upgrade:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Memory Settings&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;(JVM memory configuration has to be increased to accommodate multiple integrations with MDM)&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;- Refer to &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Installation guide&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Backup the implementation.  </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Backup the schema - Database backup&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Backup IDD application(s)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Backup customizations such as user exit code&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Backup external cleanse engine customizations&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Backup custom objects such as custom stored procedures, custom indexes etc.,&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Validate the metadata.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Resolve data issues that affect the upgrade.  </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Generate the readiness report&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Fix the data issues by running a script&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Resolve manual mandatory data issues&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;After following the best practices, proceed with the upgrade type that is applicable for your MDM implementation.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Want to know more about the upgrade types?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;0d238900-9f79-11e5-850c-bc764e10d166&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;After You Upgrade&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;The following are the list of tasks to be performed after the upgrade:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Restart the MDM Hub environment involving database, application server.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Migrate Databases to IBM DB2 with Oracle-compatibility Disabled - Refer the &lt;a title=&quot;971Upgradeguide&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/KBExternal/Pages/Home.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Upgrade guide&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for detailed steps&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update the references to Deprecated features.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Regenerate the match tokens.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Validate the upgraded metadata:   </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Validate metadata&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Resolve metadata validation messages&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run the readiness report&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Implement the updated user exit methods.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade SiperianClient library classes for the EJB protocol.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update Server properties related to Entity view and Data view&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS (if applicable):   </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Adding users to Application server for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure AVOS URNs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrading MDM workflows for AVOS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure MDM Identity service&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update Task configuration for BE based AVOS adapter&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update AVOS .BPEL files in case of custom workflows&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Sanity tests on:&amp;nbsp;   </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;IDD applications&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Hub console and batch jobs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Custom code&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;IDD - AVOS integration&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Important Note&lt;/strong&gt;: Informatica recommends that you migrate to the ActiveVOS workflow adapter based on business entities. Informatica will continue to support the Siperian workflow adapter, but it will become obsolete and Informatica will drop support in a future release.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; <div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica Data      Quality - 9.0.x, 9.1 HotFix 3, 9.5, 9.5.1, 9.6 and 9.6.1&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica      Name3 - 9.5.3 HotFix 1&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica      AddressDoctor - 5.8&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Trillium - 14      and 15&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
